      function showPopAdd() {
        var ele = document.getElementById("popAdd");	
        if(ele.style.display == "block") {
          ele.style.display = "none";		
        }
        else {
          ele.style.display = "block";

        function tickerWordsStart(){    
          currWordIndex=-1;    
          tickerWordsNextWord();    
        }    
    
        function tickerWordsNextWord(){    
          currWordIndex++;    
    
          if(currWordIndex>=words.length){    
            currWordIndex=0;    
          }    
          tickerWordsStartTickWord(currWordIndex);    
        }    
    
        function tickerWordsStartTickWord(index){    
          wordIndex=0;    
          currWord=	words[index][0];    
          currID=		words[index][1];    
    
          wordInterval=setInterval("tickerWordsAddLetter();", 100);		    
        }    
    
        function tickerWordsAddLetter(){    
          wordIndex++;    
    
          wordToDisplay=currWord.substring(0, wordIndex);    
    
          document.getElementById('headlinesTicker').innerHTML="<a href=\"http://www.ai-online.com/Adv/Previous/show_issue.php?id="+currID+"\" style=\"color: #1f65ad !important; font-weight: bold;\" target=\"_blank\">"+wordToDisplay+"</a>";    
    
          if(wordIndex>=currWord.length){    
            clearInterval(wordInterval);    
            setTimeout("tickerWordsNextWord();", 1000);    
          }    
        }    
    
        function tickerWordsPause(){    
          clearInterval(wordInterval);    
        }    
    
        function tickerWordsUnPause(){    
          wordInterval=setInterval("tickerWordsAddLetter();", 100);    
        }    
    
    
        tickerWordsStart();    
        -->    
                </script></div>
